</div>Getting your website online can seem like a daunting task  but if you follow the right steps, it can be easier than you might think. <strong>You dont need to be a web design expert</strong> with years of experience to build a great-looking website.<strong>It doesnt have to cost a fortune, either</strong>!</p>
Ive been building websites for over ten years and reviewing web hosts and website builders for almost as long.</p>
There are two ways you can build a website. <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/website-builders/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">The first option is to use a website builder</a>  a platform thats designed to make it easy for anyone to build a website, even with no previous experience or technical skills.</p>
The second way is to <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/make-free-blog-wordpress-step-step-instructions/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">use WordPress</a>. This can take a little more work, but its still pretty easy if you are technically inclined, and it gives you more flexibility. Email marketing has the power to grow your business quickly. It has a high click-through rate (CTR), too  up to 100x better than social media channels like Twitter.</p>
<div class="hightlight-paragraph hightlight-paragraph-purple">If youre short on time, you can <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=1934&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_1934_post_4_5360&post_id=4&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=post&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="1934" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_1934_post_4_5360', 'fiverr', this,  true  );"><strong>hop over to Fiverr and hire a professional web designer to build you a WordPress website for as little as $5</strong></a><strong>.</strong></div>
Im going to be exploring both options in this guide, so keep reading to find out which is the right choice for you.</p>
<h2 id="hselect--1">Option 1: Using a Website Builder</h2>
A website builder <span style="font-weight: 400;">is an online tool that</span> makes it super easy to build a website. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Website builders can be quite powerful but</span> require no coding or technical skills, <span style="font-weight: 400;">which makes them accessible to beginners</span> <span style="font-weight: 400;">and useful for professionals.</span></p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">Their intuitive interface and flexible features mean that y</span>ou can use a builder to <strong>create a website</strong>that looks great in a matter of hours  or even minutes. <strong>Most website builders are budget-friendly, and many of them offer free plans or free trials, </strong>so you can get started <span style="font-weight: 400;">without having to spend a dime</span>.</p>
Website builders come with pre-designed templates that set the style, layout, and color scheme of your site. All you have to do is pick one add your own content and images<span style="font-weight: 400;">, and personalize it with your own branding</span>.<strong></strong></p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">Depending on the</span> builder, <span style="font-weight: 400;">youll have access to</span> different methods of building and editing your site. <strong>I personally prefer drag-and-drop editing, as it gives you more control over the layout while keeping the process pretty simple.</strong> You can position elements wherever you like, or add new elements by simply dragging them into place.</p>
Some builders offer a selection of apps to choose from. This is an easy way to add functionality to your site <span style="font-weight: 400;">or integrate it with another service.</span> You can add a <span style="font-weight: 400;">mailing list</span>, an appointment booking system, a live chat box, or pretty much anything you can imagine, usually at no added cost.</p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">Though </span>there are plenty of website builders out there, <span style="font-weight: 400;">their quality greatly varies.</span> <strong>My personal favorite is Wix</strong>, as it offers hundreds of templates and great flexibility, with lots of free (and paid) apps.<strong></strong>Check out our guide to the <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/website-builders/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">best website builders</a></strong>for some other excellent choices.</p>
<h3><strong>Using a Website Builder: Step-by-Step Guide</strong></h3>
<strong>1. Decide what kind of website you want to build</strong></p>
<strong>With most website builders, you can create just about any type of website you can imagine.</strong> You may want to <strong>create a personal website</strong>, a blog, an online portfolio, or <span style="font-weight: 400;">interactive</span> a resum/CV. <span style="font-weight: 400;">If youre an entrepreneur, y</span>ou might need a website for your business, or an online store to sell your products or services.</p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">You dont even need to limit your site to</span> a single purpose. For instance, you might want to create a website for your business that also has a portfolio of your work and an online store. With the right builder, the possibilities <span style="font-weight: 400;">are only limited by your imagination.</span></p>
<strong>2. Choose the right website builder for your needs</strong></p>
Builders <span style="font-weight: 400;">will have different strengths and features</span>, so <strong>you need to <b>choose the right builder for</b> your needs.</strong> For example, while most builders <span style="font-weight: 400;">come with some sort of</span> online store <span style="font-weight: 400;">feature or add-on</span>, a builder like Shopify is specifically designed for e-commerce. On the other hand, its general-purpose features, such as blogging, are very limited.</p>
<strong><span style="font-weight: 400;">For my money, </span>the most flexible website builder is Wix. </strong>It has excellent e-commerce features, tons of apps, and its drag-and-drop editor gives you complete control over how your website looks. <b>Wix sits at the top spot of our best website builders list</b>, and Ill be using it to demonstrate the steps to building your website in this guide. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Thats not to say that its your only option though  </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">you should be able to follow these steps with most quality website builders.</span></p>
<div class="hightlight-paragraph hightlight-paragraph-purple">

Even with a free plan, you can enjoy reliable web hosting and around-the-clock maintenance and security.</li>
<li><span style="font-weight: 400;">The most beginner-friendly builder on this list, </span><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=1869&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_1869_post_4_770956&post_id=4&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=post&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="1869" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_1869_post_4_770956', 'site123', this,  true  );"><strong>SITE123 <b>offers easy and quick website building</b></strong></a>.</li>

<li><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you need to create a site for your agency that attracts clients and invites confidence,</span><b> <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=692632&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_692632_post_4_773982&post_id=4&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=post&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="692632" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_692632_post_4_773982', '1and1-ionos-hosting', this,  true  );">IONOS offers simple design with professional results</a></b><b>. </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">It also comes with easy-to-use tools for e-commerce.</span></li>

It <span style="font-weight: 400;">has hundreds of apps and tons of tools to help you boost your</span>sales.</li>

<div id="Plan"><strong>3. Choose a plan</strong></div>
Most website builders have a free plan, or at least a free trial period. If youre just getting started with your website, or if your budget is tight, a free plan can be the best solution. <strong>Free plans give you the chance to try out a website builder without investing upfront.</strong></p>
<strong>The downside, <b>however, is that</b> free plans often come with a lot of restrictions</strong>. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Youll be limited </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">to using your website builders URL (e.g., username.wixsite.com/yourcompany). Thats fine if youre creating a website as a hobby, but i</span>f youre using your website for business, you really need a custom domain name (yourcompany.com) thats easy for your customers to remember.</p>
Also, if you use a free plan your website will be full of the builders branding, which can look unprofessional.</p>
Free plans also tend to restrict the amount of traffic you can get, and <span style="font-weight: 400;">many useful features such as</span> installing apps or access<span style="font-weight: 400;">ing tools for</span> e-commerce <span style="font-weight: 400;">might be locked behind a paywall</span>. <strong>If youre serious about your website, youll likely need to upgrade to a paid plan.</strong></p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">Its important that you</span>know the type of website you want to build <span style="font-weight: 400;">before choosing a plan. That way, you</span> can select a plan <span style="font-weight: 400;">thats better suited</span> to both your budget and your needs. For example:</p>
<ul>
<li>If you want to sell online, <span style="font-weight: 400;">youll probably want to go for</span> a designated business plan (or, <span style="font-weight: 400;">at the very least, </span> a plan <span style="font-weight: 400;">with the necessary tools for</span> e-commerce). Wix has general and business/e-commerce plans to choose from, but you can only accept online payments on the business/e-commerce plans.</li>
<li>If you want to<span style="font-weight: 400;">showcase your work by</span> hosting a lot of videos <span style="font-weight: 400;">or high-resolution images</span> on your website, youll need a plan with a lot of storage and bandwidth. For instance, Squarespace gives you unlimited photo storage on every plan, including its cheapest.</li>
</ul>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">I recommend going for </span> the lowest-priced plan that gives you all the features you need right now. <span style="font-weight: 400;">If your needs change,</span> you can always upgrade to a higher-priced plan in the future.</p>
<strong>4. Get started: Choose a template</strong></p>
The first step in the process <span style="font-weight: 400;">will always be choosing a template</span>. All website builders use templates (some builders call them themes, but they mean the same thing) as the building blocks of your website. <strong>Templates are professionally designed to work on all types of devices, </strong>and they allow you to get your website online in a relatively short amount of time.</p>
The template sets the style and general layout of your website (although you can customize it later), providing you with a framework that you can <span style="font-weight: 400;">customize and use to add your own content.</span></p>
<strong>Most website builders have template libraries that you can browse even before you sign up.</strong> Templates are arranged in categories, as you can see in the screenshot from <strong>Wixs template gallery</strong>. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Categories arent meant to be restrictive (its not that you </span><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">cant</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;"> use a portfolio template for your blog),</span> but each category contains templates that are specifically <span style="font-weight: 400;">designed </span> for different types of websites.</p>
The best templates look fantastic right out of the box. As far as I&#8217;m concerned, Squarespace has some of the most visually stunning templates out there.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3225434" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3225434"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:53.25% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/updated-homepage-images-jan-2024--1.png"  width="1600" height="852" alt="Wix Template Gallery" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/updated-homepage-images-jan-2024--1.png"   width="1600" height="852" alt="Wix Template Gallery" class="border wp-image-3225434 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3225434"class="wp-caption-text">Choose the template that best matches your vision</figcaption></figure>
<strong>5. Customize your template</strong></p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">Technically, y</span>ou dont <i>have</i> to make any customizations to your website template once youve chosen it  but <span style="font-weight: 400;">regardless of how well-crafted a template is,</span> customizing your website <span style="font-weight: 400;">is what truly makes it</span> your own and sets it apart from other websites <span style="font-weight: 400;">(especially those using the exact same template).</span> <b>A good place to start would be changing your templates</b><strong> colors and fonts to match your business branding.</strong></p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">Although different builders will give you varied </span><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">levels</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;"> of customization, one of the huge advantages of using a builder is that they make customization</span> rather easy. While each website builder will have <span style="font-weight: 400;">its own unique</span> editor, <span style="font-weight: 400;">everything Im about</span> to demonstrate in Wix <span style="font-weight: 400;">can be accomplished through similar steps in other</span> builders.</p>
<h4 id="h.ijyj76kxh923" class="c4"><strong>Changing fonts </strong></h4>
<strong>Changing the fonts on Wix is simply a matter of clicking on the text you want to change and hitting the </strong><i><strong>Edit Text</strong></i><strong>button.</strong>You can edit each text box separately or use the <i>Save Theme</i>option to apply your font changes across your whole website.</p>
With Wix, you can choose different fonts for different text types  for instance, you can choose one font for <i>Heading 1</i> to use as your main heading <span style="font-weight: 400;">(like in the template Im demonstrating below)</span><span style="font-weight: 400;">,</span> and another font for <span style="font-weight: 400;">your</span> sub-headings. You can even have a different font for paragraph styles, if you like.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3225463" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3225463"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:51.333333333333% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/updated-homepage-images-jan-2024--2.png"  width="1500" height="770" alt="Wix Text Editing" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/updated-homepage-images-jan-2024--2.png"   width="1500" height="770" alt="Wix Text Editing" class="border wp-image-3225463 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3225463"class="wp-caption-text">Wix gives you an amazing level of customization over global text styles</figcaption></figure>
Some website builders only allow you to change the font style for the whole website, rather than for individual headings <span style="font-weight: 400;">and paragraphs</span>. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Though that limits your options somewhat,</span> Id recommend you keep a consistent style throughout your website anyway.</p>
<h4 id="h.73hfz06o8r9w" class="c4"><strong>Changing colors </strong></h4>
You can easily change the color of your fonts in the text settings box, but its just as easy to change the color of other elements, like backgrounds of columns. For example, you can use a solid color background using the color picker tool as demonstrated in the screenshot below.</p>
<strong>Wix <b>automatically creates</b> complementary color palettes to match your theme, but you can change the palettes by using the change your site colors option.</strong>You can also add your own colors to match your branding.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3225492" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3225492"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:50.333333333333% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/updated-homepage-images-jan-2024--3.png"  width="1500" height="755" alt="Changing Background Color Wix" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/updated-homepage-images-jan-2024--3.png"   width="1500" height="755" alt="Changing Background Color Wix" class="border wp-image-3225492 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3225492"class="wp-caption-text">Wix has easy options for changing colors and backgrounds</figcaption></figure>
<h4 id="h.a7625ks0uxmo" class="c4"><strong>Moving elements around on your pages </strong></h4>
<strong>Drag-and-drop editors make rearranging <b>your pages</b> content <b>a simple </b>matter of, well, dragging it from one place to another. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Wix is unique in the amount of control it gives you over arranging your pages layout, but</span></strong>other drag-and-drop editors <span style="font-weight: 400;">will give you similar features.</span></p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">Other</span> editors may offer an up/down button method for moving sections around on your web page. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Block editors work like a middle point between the two, with pre-made blocks (text, image, video, columns, etc.) that you can arrange in a grid, giving you more flexibility than just moving content up or down, but not as much room to play around with as a drag-and-drop editor.</span></p>
One <span style="font-weight: 400;">thing that I particularly like about</span> Wix is the <i>Zoom Out and Reorder</i>function. <strong>This allows you to view your whole web page and easily move sections and/or elements around on the page.</strong> Below<span style="font-weight: 400;">, you can see</span> how easy it is to move content using this tool.</p>
<figure id="attachment_2811583" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-2811583"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:46.3125% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/image-1.gif"  width="1600" height="741" alt="image-1.gif" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/image-1.gif"   width="1600" height="741" alt="image-1.gif" class="wp-image-2811583 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-2811583"class="wp-caption-text">Using Wixs drag-and-drop editor to rearrange sections</figcaption></figure>
<strong>6. Add your own content</strong></p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">When it comes to </span>adding your own content<span style="font-weight: 400;">, all you have to do </span>is <span style="font-weight: 400;">replace</span> the placeholder text and images in your template with your own text and media. <span style="font-weight: 400;">It might take some time</span>if you have a lot of content, <span style="font-weight: 400;">but the overall process is really simple.</span></p>
If you dont have your own images, most website builders offer some kind of image bank that allows you to instantly add free images to your site.</p>
<p id="h.qmentnxq8eef" class="c4"><strong>How to add text</strong><br />
<strong>You can add new text sections to your web pages in just a few clicks.</strong>In Wix, you use the <i>Add</i>tool in the toolbar on the left and then select <i>Text</i>in the pop-out menu.</p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">I recommend</span> setting up the main areas <span style="font-weight: 400;">where you want to add text first </span>and <span style="font-weight: 400;">then going back to</span> add your content. You can use our free <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/webtools/lorem-ipsum/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Lorem Ipsum Generator</a></strong> to create placeholder text to use until youre ready to add your own text.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3114324" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3114324"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:43.75% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-4.png"  width="1600" height="700" alt="Wix Text Styles" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-4.png"   width="1600" height="700" alt="Wix Text Styles" class="border wp-image-3114324 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3114324"class="wp-caption-text">Choose from a wide variety of text styles</figcaption></figure>
<p id="h.2da1l3utaiwk" class="c4"><strong>How to add an image</strong><br />
Like adding text to your website, adding images is incredibly easy. In Wix, open the <i>Add</i>menu, select <i>Image</i>(directly below <i>Text</i>), and choose from the range of image sources. You can upload your own images, use free Wix images and illustrations, search the Unsplash images database, or choose premium stock images from Shutterstock (for an added fee). Then, <span style="font-weight: 400;">all you have to do is </span>place the image where you want it on your page.</p>
You can also use the <i>Add Image</i> tool to add a logo to your website. Ive got some advice about logos <a href="#logo" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'logo', this,  );">further on in this article</a>.</p>
If youre using free Wix or Unsplash images, these may be already optimized &#8211; meaning that theyve been compressed to smaller file size so that they wont slow your website down. If youre using your own <span style="font-weight: 400;">high-resolution</span> images, however, its a good idea to reduce the file sizes before you upload them. <strong>Thats easy to do with a free tool such as our </strong><strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/webtools/imagecompressor/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Image Compressor</a></strong><strong>.</strong></p>
<figure id="attachment_3114353" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3114353"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:45.25% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-5.png"  width="1600" height="724" alt="Free Wix Images" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-5.png"   width="1600" height="724" alt="Free Wix Images" class="border wp-image-3114353 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3114353"class="wp-caption-text">Wix offers multiple ways of adding images to your website</figcaption></figure>
<p id="h.r52c5tstcoac" class="c4"><strong>How to add a page to your website</strong><br />
Most templates will come with several pre-designed pages, such as <i>Home</i>, <i>About Us</i>, and <i>Contact</i>. If you want to add more pages &#8211; a <i>Services <span style="font-weight: 400;">or </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">My Work </span></i> page,for example &#8211; you can do this by clicking the <i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Menus and Pages</span></i> button <span style="font-weight: 400;">on the left</span> toolbar and selecting the <i>Add Page</i>button at the bottom of the pop-out menu.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3114382" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3114382"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:51.75% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-6.png"  width="1600" height="828" alt="Pages and Menus" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-6.png"   width="1600" height="828" alt="Pages and Menus" class="border wp-image-3114382 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3114382"class="wp-caption-text">Adding a new page in Wix couldnt be easier</figcaption></figure>
When you add a new page to your site, it will automatically show up in your navigation menu.</p>
<strong>7. Add apps</strong></p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">Apps are third-party or native integrations that help expand the functionality of your site. Although n</span>ot all website builders have apps, some <strong>builders like</strong> <strong>Wix have hundreds of apps to choose from</strong>. Many of them are free, and even the paid apps <span style="font-weight: 400;">often come with a free version or a free trial period</span>.</p>
You can use apps to add extra features to your website in a matter of minutes. For instance, <span style="font-weight: 400;">Wixs app market allows</span> you to add features like online booking, live chat, newsletter signup, social media integration, and much more to your site.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3114411" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3114411"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:47.6875% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-7.png"  width="1600" height="763" alt="Wix App Store" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-7.png"   width="1600" height="763" alt="Wix App Store" class="border wp-image-3114411 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3114411"class="wp-caption-text">The Wix app market offers hundreds of options to expand your sites functionality</figcaption></figure>
<strong><b>To add apps to your Wix site j</b>ust click the </strong><i><strong>App Market</strong></i><strong> icon (<b>it should appear as four small squares on the left toolbar</b></strong><strong>).</strong> From here, you can search for a specific app, or browse the categories to find new ideas.</p>
Once youve found an app you like, just click on it, and then select<i> Add to Site.</i></p>
<figure id="attachment_3114440" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3114440"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:43.125% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-8.png"  width="1600" height="690" alt="Wix Add App to Site" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/untitled-document-8.png"   width="1600" height="690" alt="Wix Add App to Site" class="border wp-image-3114440 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3114440"class="wp-caption-text">With a couple of clicks, install apps directly from Wix App Market</figcaption></figure>
Once the app is installed, its immediately available on your web page. In this example, I added the <i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Rollover Image Effects</span></i> app for <span style="font-weight: 400;">advanced image editing and it was available</span> on my webpage within 30 seconds!</p>
<strong>8. Choose a domain name</strong></p>
Before you publish your website, youll need to choose a domain name. If youre on a free plan, <a href="#Plan" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'plan', this,  );">you&#8217;ll have to use a sub-domain</a> (e.g. yourusername.wixsites.com/yourwebsitename). <strong>If you sign up for an annual paid plan, most builders will include a free custom domain name for the first year.</strong></p>
<strong>Most website builders <b>will give you the option of registering</b> and setting up <b>your domain name. </b></strong>That means that all you have to worry about is choosing the best domain name for your website. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Having the right domain name is absolutely crucial though</span>, so dont rush this step! <span style="font-weight: 400;">Even with the perfect name in mind,</span> one of the biggest issues <span style="font-weight: 400;">youll have to deal with</span> is whether the domain name you want is actually available.</p>
<strong><b>If youre having trouble deciding, check out our</b></strong><strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/ultimate-guide-to-choosing-a-domain-name/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">complete guide to choosing your domain name</a>!</strong></p>
<strong>9. Preview and publish your website</strong></p>
Now that youve added all your content and chosen your domain name, its time to get your website online. With most website builders, this is really just a matter of clicking a button (or two).</p>
<strong>Don&#8217;t rush to hit the </strong><i><strong>Publish</strong></i><strong> button yet  its always a good idea to use the </strong><i><strong>Preview</strong></i><strong> option to make sure youre happy with your site before going live. </strong>Previewing allows you to see your site the same way your visitors will, without the distractions of the editor. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Besides, if theres any spot where you forgot to add your content, or any blank pages you forgot to fill, previewing your site can help you catch those small details before anyone else does. </span></p>
Most builders will also let you preview the mobile version of your site. <b>Always make sure that your site works and looks good on mobile devices too.</b></p>
<figure id="attachment_2812096" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-2812096"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-smallimg-wrapper " style="max-width: 780px"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:42.564102564103% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/loko_optimized-optimage1.png"  width="780" height="332" alt="loko_optimized" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/loko_optimized-optimage1.png"   width="780" height="332" alt="loko_optimized" class="size-full wp-image-2812096 ll-img"/></span></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-2812096"class="wp-caption-text">When your website is published, you can easily view and share it</figcaption></figure>
Once you hit <i>Publish</i>, your website is live, and you can start promoting it!</p>

<h2 id="hselect--3"><strong>Website Builder FAQ</strong></h2>
<strong></p>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Which website builder is the easiest to use?</h3>
</strong><span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">There are several website builders that are very easy to use, such as <span style="font-weight: 400;">IONOS</span> and <strong>SITE123</strong>. However, <strong>Wix is my top choice</strong><span style="font-weight: 400;">because it manages to give you a ton of design </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">freedom</span><span style="font-weight: 400;"> while still being impressively easy to use. Not only is it incredibly intuitive, but it also has more features than almost any other builder.</span></span><strong></p>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Will my site appear on Google and other search engines?</h3>
</strong><span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Yes, your website will show up in search engine results. <span style="font-weight: 400;">But its not enough to just show up  you also want your site to rank as highly as possible.</span> All website builders offer <span style="font-weight: 400;">SEO (search engine optimization)</span> features to help improve your <span style="font-weight: 400;">search result ranking</span>.</p>
In some cases, youre limited to adding your own meta titles and descriptions. Other website builders, however, will give you more advanced SEO features. For example, Wix offers an SEO Wiz, <span style="font-weight: 400;">which</span>gives you personalized SEO recommendations and step-by-step instructions on how to get your website noticed.</span><strong></p>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Will my site look good on mobile devices?</h3>
</strong><span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">The simple answer to this question is yes. Most website builders either give you options for mobile-responsive templates (meaning your site will automatically adjust to the screen size of mobile devices) or have a mobile view editor so you can edit the mobile version of your website separately. If you want to check that your website is mobile-responsive, you can use <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/webtools/responsive-checker/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">our free Responsive Checker Tool</a>.</strong></span><strong></p>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Do I need a dedicated e-commerce builder?</h3>
</strong><span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">It really depends on how many products you plan on selling and<span style="font-weight: 400;">the main purpose of your website. For a regular blog that sells merchandise on the side,</span> a regular website builder with e-commerce features is <span style="font-weight: 400;">more than enough</span>.</p>
Thats because e-commerce builders are generally so focused on selling that their blogging tools arent all that great. <strong>Wix gives you the best of both worlds</strong><strong>, </strong>with great tools for creating content <i>and</i>a strong set of e-commerce tools.</p>
However, if youre planning to sell a lot of products through your own online store, then Id definitely recommend a dedicated e-commerce builder like <strong>Shopify</strong>. E-commerce builders have more powerful sales management tools, and some even let you sell via Instagram and Facebook as well.</span><strong></p>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Can I hire someone to build my site for me?</h3>
</strong><span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Yes, you certainly can! If you dont have the time to build your own website or youd just rather have a professional take care of it for you, you can<strong> hire a web designer for as little as $5 on Fiverr</strong>, the best marketplace for finding low-cost freelancers.</span></p>
<h2 id="hselect--4">Option 2: Using WordPress</h2>
Website builders are absolutely the easiest way to get your website online, but they can be a little more expensive than using WordPress with a web hosting plan. <strong>If youre looking for a budget-friendly option and you dont mind a slightly more technical site-building process, then WordPress <b>might be the choice for you.</b></strong></p>
Now, there are two versions of WordPress: <strong>WordPress.com</strong>, which is a simplified version, and self-hosted WordPress.org. In this section, Ill be discussing self-hosted WordPress.</p>
<strong>WordPress isnt quite as simple to use as a website builder, but its still pretty easy to get started with</strong>  and its massive range of free templates and plugins give you almost limitless options for customizing your website. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Though the process is a bit more technical,</span> you dont need to know how to code or have a lot of experience to build a great-looking website with WordPress.</p>
<div class="hightlight-paragraph hightlight-paragraph-purple">If youd rather have a professional build your WordPress website for you, then you can always <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=1934&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_1934_post_4_5388&post_id=4&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=post&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="1934" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_1934_post_4_5388', 'fiverr', this,  true  );"><strong>hire a developer on Fiverr for as little as $5</strong></a><strong>.</strong>Find out more about this below.</div>
<h3><strong>Step-by-Step Guide</strong></h3>
<strong>1. Choose a hosting plan</strong></p>
<strong>Although WordPress itself is 100% free, youll have to sign up for web hosting <b>to make your website available online</b> </strong>(unlike with website builders that provide hosting with their plans). For <span style="font-weight: 400;">a more in-depth look</span>, you can check out our shortlist of the <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/web-hosting/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">best web hosts</a> in 2024.</strong></p>
There are lots of web hosting options available  but <span style="font-weight: 400;">here are the ones that consistently top our recommendations.</span></p>
<div class="hightlight-paragraph hightlight-paragraph-purple">
<p id="h.r7usp74x9l0z" class="c4"><strong>Our Top Web Host Recommendations for WordPress Websites</strong></p>
<ul>

<strong>When youre choosing a host for your WordPress website, there are some features you should look for:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><strong>SSL certificate. </strong>An SSL certificate makes your website secure, ensuring your site has the little padlock icon in the address bar of web browsers. Most web hosts will include one for free. Once your website is live, you can check that the SSL certificate on your website is working properly with the <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/webtools/ssl-checker/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">SSL Checker Tool</a>.</strong></li>
<li><strong>WordPress optimization. </strong>The best web hosts for WordPress have specially optimized servers to improve performance, so your web pages load faster.</li>
<li><strong>Security features. </strong>Some web hosts charge you extra for essential security, so you should try to find one that includes important features such as malware protection, firewalls, and automatic backups.</li>
</ul>
<strong>2. Choose a domain name</strong></p>
This process is pretty much the same<span style="font-weight: 400;">for using WordPress as it is</span> for website builders. Some web hosts include free domain names with annual plans, but not all do. <strong>If you choose a host that doesnt offer a free domain name, it may be cheaper to buy your domain name from a third party rather than through your web host. </strong>You can pick up a domain name for as little as $1 on some domain marketplaces.</p>
<strong>3. Use a one-click installer to install WordPress</strong></p>
Some hosting plans come with WordPress pre-installed. If your plan doesnt, dont panic &#8211; you can use the one-click installer provided by your host.</p>
<span style="font-weight: 400;">One-click might be a bit of a misnomer,</span> <span style="font-weight: 400;">but its not too far off  </span>with just a few clicks, <span style="font-weight: 400;">these tools</span> set up all the scripts and databases needed to make WordPress work on your website. <strong>All you really have to do is <b>come up with </b>a username and password that you want to use to log in to WordPress once the installation is complete.</strong></p>
Different hosts may use different one-click installers, but essentially theyre all the same, and theyre all very easy to use.</p>
<figure id="attachment_1565959" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1565959"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:88.694127957932% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/installing-wordpress-via-siteground.png"  width="1141" height="1012" alt="installing wordpress via siteground" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/installing-wordpress-via-siteground.png"   width="1141" height="1012" alt="installing wordpress via siteground" class="wp-image-1565959 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1565959"class="wp-caption-text">Most WordPress installers will be similar to this one from SiteGround</figcaption></figure>
<strong>4. Access WordPress through your hosting dashboard</strong></p>
The exact way youll access WordPress may vary depending on your web host. In most cases, however,<strong> youll find the option for managing your WordPress website <b>in your hosting dashboard</b>.</strong></p>
Ill be demonstrating this using SiteGround. In the screenshot below, you can see that theres a button to automatically log in to my WordPress websites dashboard. Other hosts might make you type in your WordPress username and password to log in.</p>
<figure id="attachment_1565994" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1565994"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:74.029640084686% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/SiteGround-offers-a-one-click-login-option-for-your-WordPress-dashboard.png"  width="1417" height="1049" alt="installing wordpress via siteground" /></noscript><img data-src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/SiteGround-offers-a-one-click-login-option-for-your-WordPress-dashboard.png"   width="1417" height="1049" alt="installing wordpress via siteground" class="wp-image-1565994 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1565994"class="wp-caption-text">SiteGround offers a one-click login option for your WordPress dashboard</figcaption></figure>
<strong><b>If this is your first time using</b> WordPress, the dashboard may seem a little overwhelming, but <b>dont panic,</b> its actually quite easy to navigate. </strong>Below is a screenshot of the dashboard with all the important elements labeled for you.</p>
<figure id="attachment_2812131" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-2812131"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-smallimg-wrapper " style="max-width: 780px"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:54.230769230769% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/moko_optimized-optimage1.png"  width="780" height="423" alt="moko_optimized" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/moko_optimized-optimage1.png"   width="780" height="423" alt="moko_optimized" class="border wp-image-2812131 size-full ll-img"/></span></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-2812131"class="wp-caption-text">The WordPress dashboard is easy to navigate once you know where everything is!</figcaption></figure>
WordPress uses some jargon thats different from website builders, so to make things easy, heres a brief rundown of the different sections of the WordPress dashboard:</p>

<strong>5. Choose a theme</strong></p>
<strong>Themes in WordPress are very similar to templates in website builders. </strong>The biggest difference is that in WordPress, themes control more than just the general style/layout of your website. A particular theme can often include certan plugins (or required plugins.)</p>
<figure id="attachment_2812160" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-2812160"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-smallimg-wrapper " style="max-width: 780px"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:52.179487179487% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/kkk_optimized-optimage1.png"  width="780" height="407" alt="kkk_optimized" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/kkk_optimized-optimage1.png"   width="780" height="407" alt="kkk_optimized" class="size-full wp-image-2812160 ll-img"/></span></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-2812160"class="wp-caption-text">In the themes panel, view all the themes you have installed</figcaption></figure>
WordPress&#8217; <span style="font-weight: 400;">default theme</span> is pretty basic, so youre probably going to want to <span style="font-weight: 400;">look for a different one</span>. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Thankfully,</span> the WordPress theme installer <span style="font-weight: 400;">makes this extremely easy</span>. <strong>You can search the WordPress theme repository <b>to find and</b> install any of the thousands of free themes available <b>in an instant</b>. </strong>You can even install multiple themes and use the customizer to see how they will look on your website before activating them.</p>
<figure id="attachment_1566083" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:45.784418356457% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/WordPress-repository.png"  width="1874" height="858" alt="WordPress repository" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/WordPress-repository.png"   width="1874" height="858" alt="WordPress repository" class="border wp-image-1566083 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption-text">Search for, install, and activate free themes from the WordPress repository</figcaption></figure>
In addition to the free themes offered by WordPress, you can purchase thousands of premium third-party themes from marketplaces like <strong>TemplateMonster</strong><strong></strong>and <strong>ThemeForest</strong>.</p>
<strong>6. Add plugins </strong></p>
Plugins are similar to the apps offered by website builders  <strong>they add extra features to your website that arent included in WordPress itself. </strong>For example, you can install a plugin to create a contact form (e.g., NinjaForms) or build an online store using WooCommerce. Chances are, if you can think of a feature, there&#8217;s a plugin for it, from SEO to creating an online portfolio.</p>
<figure id="attachment_1566083" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:34.917245061399% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/manage-your-installed-plugins-in-WordPress.png"  width="1873" height="654" alt="manage your installed plugins in WordPress" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/manage-your-installed-plugins-in-WordPress.png"   width="1873" height="654" alt="manage your installed plugins in WordPress" class="wp-image-1566112 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption-text">You can even install multiple</figcaption></figure>
<strong>Use the search box to help you find the plugins you need. </strong> There, youll also find information about each plugin, including whether its compatible with your version of WordPress, what features it has, and what other users think about it.</p>
<figure id="attachment_1566083" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:34.670947030498% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Find-and-install-plugins-easily-in-WordPress.png"  width="1869" height="648" alt="Install plugins" /></noscript><img data-src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Find-and-install-plugins-easily-in-WordPress.png"   width="1869" height="648" alt="Install plugins" class="wp-image-1566141 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption-text">Find and install plugins easily in WordPress</figcaption></figure>
It only takes a single click to install a plugin, but your plugins will only work on your website when you have clicked the activate button in the plugins panel.</p>
<strong>7. Create your first post</strong></p>
One of the most frequent questions I get asked about WordPress is regarding the difference between pages and posts. Essentially, pages are the static content &#8211; i.e., the content on your website that doesnt change or doesnt change very often, such as an <i>About Us</i>page. Posts are more dynamic  they show up on the blog page or category pages of your website. <strong>The key difference between pages and posts is in the way WordPress displays them on your site.</strong></p>
The editor for creating posts and pages is exactly the same, so the process for creating pages and posts is identical. In the screenshot below, you can see that when you click on the posts panel of the dashboard, youll see a list of your existing posts (some themes come with demo content), with an <i>Add New</i>button at the top.</p>
<figure id="attachment_1566083" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:48.021390374332% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/The-posts-panel-in-WordPress.png"  width="1870" height="898" alt="The posts" /></noscript><img data-src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/The-posts-panel-in-WordPress.png"   width="1870" height="898" alt="The posts" class="wp-image-1566170 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption-text">The posts panel in WordPress</figcaption></figure>
Clicking the <i>Add New</i>button will take you to the editor. WordPresss default editor used to be pretty basic, but the Gutenberg version that was introduced with WordPress 5.0, along with the new features of 6.0, give you much more flexibility. <strong>Gutenberg uses blocks to create your posts and pages, along with layouts (columns), sections, and containers.</strong></p>
Using free plugins, you have the option to add more blocks to the Gutenberg editor. Additionally, third-party site-building plugins allow you to alter the way you edit your site.</p>
<figure id="attachment_1566083" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:44.569892473118% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Gutenberg-block-plugins-for-WordPress.png"  width="1860" height="829" alt="Gutenberg block plugins for WordPress" /></noscript><img data-src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Gutenberg-block-plugins-for-WordPress.png"   width="1860" height="829" alt="Gutenberg block plugins for WordPress" class="wp-image-1566199 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption-text">Gutenberg block plugins expand the features of the WordPress editor</figcaption></figure>
Block types included in the standard Gutenberg editor include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Paragraph</li>
<li>Heading</li>
<li>Quote</li>
<li>Image</li>
<li>List</li>
<li>Cover image</li>
<li>Gallery</li>
<li>Slideshow</li>
<li>Table</li>
<li>Buttons</li>
</ul>
To choose a block, you can click the + icon at the side of each paragraph area or type / into the free space labeled start writing or type / to choose block.</p>
<figure id="attachment_1566083" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:63.179916317992% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/The-post-and-page-editor-in-WordPress.png"  width="1434" height="906" alt="Page editor" /></noscript><img data-src="https://images.websiteplanet.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/The-post-and-page-editor-in-WordPress.png"   width="1434" height="906" alt="Page editor" class="border wp-image-1566228 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption-text">The post and page editor in WordPress</figcaption></figure>
<strong>8. Publish your site</strong></p>
Unlike some website builders (such as <strong>Wix</strong>), WordPress doesnt have a specific <i>Publish</i>button for your whole website. <strong>As soon as you create your WordPress website, its live on the internet.</strong>However, there are three separate places where youll find <i>Publish</i>buttons in WordPress.</p>
These are:</p>
<ul>
<li>In the customizer, where youll see a button at the top of the panel which saves changes and makes your customizations live.</li>
<li>At the top right of each new post you create, you will find the option to publish. Until you click publish, your post will remain a draft and won&#8217;t be visible to others. If you decide to make edits later on, simply click update to make your changes go live.</li>
<li>At the top right of each new page you create. As with posts, your content is just a draft until you publish, and when you make edits you need to click update or your changes wont be saved.</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_1566083" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:64.795607077486% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/publishing-your-website-in-WordPress.png"  width="1639" height="1062" alt="Publishing your website in WordPress" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/publishing-your-website-in-WordPress.png"   width="1639" height="1062" alt="Publishing your website in WordPress" class="border wp-image-1566259 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption-text">The three areas where you need to click publish in WordPress</figcaption></figure>

If youre short on time or just dont want to deal with any problems that could occur when building a WordPress website, <strong>then hiring a professional to build (and, perhaps, maintain) your website could be a better choice.</strong></p>
Hiring a developer sure sounds expensive, but thanks to the rise of freelance platforms like Fiverr, you dont have to spend a small fortune. I just did a quick search on Fiverr for full WordPress website creation and found <strong>plenty of professional website designers offering to build your website for as little as $5!</strong></p>
<figure id="attachment_1566083" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:82.106096595408% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/low-cost-developers-on-Fiverr.png"  width="1263" height="1037" alt="Low-cost web developers on Fiverr" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/low-cost-developers-on-Fiverr.png"   width="1263" height="1037" alt="Low-cost web developers on Fiverr" class="border wp-image-1566288 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1566083"class="wp-caption-text">Low-cost web developers on Fiverr for as little as $5</figcaption></figure>
One of the great features of Fiverr is that it allows you to view samples of a designer&#8217;s work to see if they are a good match for the kind of website you need. Moreover, Fiverr ensures you&#8217;re completely safe because the platform holds back your payment to the freelancer until you&#8217;re pleased with their work.</p>

<h2 id="hselect--5"><strong>WordPress FAQ</strong></h2>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"><strong>Is WordPress free?</strong></h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Technically, yes. The platform itself is 100% free, but you will have to pay for web hosting and a domain name (<a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/web-hosting/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>click here for a list of the best web hosts in 2024</strong></a>). If you want a premium theme or plugin from a third-party marketplace, youll have to pay a fee for these, too.</span></p>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"><strong>Can I build a WordPress site on my own?</strong></h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Yes, you can build a WordPress website without hiring a developer  but if youre new to website building, <strong>youll probably find Wix much easier (and faster) to use</strong>. WordPress is more complex and its easier to mess up your website when making changes to settings or by installing plugins that conflict with one another.<br />
Hiring a developer for your WordPress website isnt as expensive as it sounds! You can actually <strong>find a developer to meet any budget on Fiverr</strong>.</span></p>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"><strong>Whats the difference between WordPress.com and WordPress.org?</strong></h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">The main difference between WordPress.com and WordPress.org is in the way theyre hosted. With <strong>WordPress.com</strong>, you dont have to pay separately for hosting but you will need to upgrade to one of the highest-priced plans (Business or eCommerce) to use plugins and upload themes from third-party marketplaces.<br />
WordPress.org is self-hosted, so you pay for hosting separately. You have complete control and freedom with this version and it can work out much cheaper than WordPress.com.</span></p>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"><strong>What is better, Wix, or WordPress?</strong></h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">There are pros and cons to both Wix and WordPress. <strong>Wix is more beginner-friendly</strong>but it can cost more than buying a hosting plan and building your site with WordPress.<br />
WordPress gives you a lot of flexibility and gives you more options for growing your site over time, but it can be trickier to learn and theres potentially more that can go wrong. For example, incompatible plugins can cause your website to stop working.</span></p>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"><strong>Do I need a special WordPress hosting plan, or is a basic hosting plan enough?</strong></h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline"><strong>You dont <em>need</em> a special WordPress hosting plan, as WordPress will work on any shared hosting plan that has a one-click installer.</strong> However, there are definite benefits to choosing a WordPress-specific hosting plan.<br />
WordPress-specific hosting plans can be managed or unmanaged. With unmanaged plans, your hosting is pretty much the same as basic hosting, but your website will be hosted on servers that are optimized for WordPress and you might get access to some optimization plugins.<br />
Managed WordPress hosting is the hassle-free version, as your host takes care of things like updates, security patching (depending on the host), and backups, so you can just get on with building your website. See our list of the <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/best-managed-wordpress-hosting/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>best managed WordPress hosting providers in 2024</strong></a>.</span></p>
<h2 id="hselect--6">Taking Your Website to the Next Level</h2>
Now youve built your website, its time to get it noticed. In my experience, youre never completely finished with building a website, since you can always keep updating it, changing things and making it better. <strong>You want people to start visiting your website as soon as possible. </strong>Luckily, there are a number of things that you can doto grow your audience and give your site visitors a better experience.</p>
<h3><div id="logo">Designing a Logo</div></h3>
You dont need to have a logo before you start building your website, but <strong>a logo makes your website look more professional</strong>and can help build your brand.</p>
Your logo says a lot about you, so its important to take time to get it right. There are design trends to take into consideration &#8211; for instance, have you thought about the impact your color scheme can have on your target audience? Read more about the <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/logo-design-stats/">latest logo statistics from the Fortune 500 list</a></strong>to explore this further.</p>
There are two ways to get yourself a logo  and both are affordable. My colleague actually tested all the major logo design services to find a new logo for Website Planet. To read all about his experiment and see who won, read our full comparison of the <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/logo-design-services/">best online logo design services</a></strong>.</p>
<strong>1. Do It Yourself with an Online Logo Maker</strong></p>
The DIY method may sound like the cheapest way to get a logo  but this isnt always the case. <strong>Most online logo makers are free to try, but you will have to pay to download and use your logo.</strong>There are a few free logo makers out there, but theyre very basic and I dont recommend using them.</p>
My favorite of all DIY logo makers is <strong>Wix Logo Maker</strong>. This tool uses AI (artificial intelligence) to generate lots of logo ideas based on your own personal preferences. When you spot a design you like, you can customize everything from the fonts to the color scheme. You can even download a free low-res version of your logo so you can see how it might look on your website and social media before you make your final purchase.</p>
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=852837&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_852837_post_4_5417&post_id=4&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=post&amp=0" data-id="852837" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_852837_post_4_5417', 'wix-logo-maker', this,  true  );">Try Wix Logo Maker for Free &gt;&gt;</a></div>
<strong>2. Hire a Designer</strong></p>
Hiring a logo designer might sound expensive &#8211; <strong>but on Fiverr, you can get a professionally designed logo for as little as $5</strong><strong>.</strong>Most Fiverr designers display examples of logos theyve created, making it easier to find someone who offers the style youre looking for. <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/logo-design-services/fiverr-logo-design/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">We tested Fiverrs logo designers ourselves</a></strong>and were really impressed with the quality of the finished logos.</p>
In addition to your logo, youll also need to generate a favicon  this is the small image that you usually see in browser tabs next to the website name and in your bookmarks. You can create a favicon in seconds with our <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/webtools/favicon-generator/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">nifty favicon generator tool</a></strong>.</p>
<h3><strong>Optimizing Your Site</strong></h3>
Even if you build a fabulous website, its not going to show up on the first page of search engine results pages (SERPs) without some optimization. <strong>Optimizing your website involves search engine optimization (SEO), analyzing your traffic, and understanding what your audience is looking for.</strong></p>
For SEO, there are some great tools that you can use to make optimization easier. One of the best tools available is SEMrush (check out our <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/semrush-review/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>Guide to SEMrush</strong></a>to find out more), but there are other options if SEMrush is out of your budget. Weve reviewed some of the <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/seo-tools-for-content-marketers/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>best SEO Tools</strong></a>to help you choose the right one.</p>
Creating the right content for your website might seem like a challenge, but by using analytics tools to find out more about your audience (where they live, their age, their gender, and so on), you can tailor your content better. Read our <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/ultimate-beginners-guide-google-analytics/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Guide to Google Analytics</a></strong>to see how to get the most out of analytics tools. You can also use tools like Answer the Public to find out what people are searching for. Check out our <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/ultimate-guide-answer-public-go-pro/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Guide to Answer the Public</a></strong>for more about this.</p>
<h3><strong>Grow Your Audience with Email Marketing</strong></h3>
<strong>Email marketing is one of the best ways to grow your audience </strong> and there are lots of tools to help you succeed with your marketing efforts.</p>
Email marketing possesses the ability to rapidly expand your business. Additionally, it exhibits a high click-through rate (CTR), surpassing social media channels like Twitter by up to 100 times. Through email marketing, you can provide customers with enticing discounts and promotions, encourage them to share your business with others, and offer valuable free resources to entice visitors into signing up for your mailing list.</p>
To get the most out of email marketing, youll need to think about the frequency of your emails, using automated emails, and what to put in your email newsletters. <strong>For more tips, check out our </strong><strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/email-marketing-stats-need-know/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">collection of the most important email marketing stats</a></strong><strong>.</strong></p>
We have tested and reviewed the <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/email-marketing-services/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">best email marketing platforms</a></strong>. No time to read a bunch of reviews? No worries, heres a quick overview of our favorite email marketing solutions.</p>
<ul>
<li>ActiveCampaign  This is, hands down, the most feature-packed email marketing service on the market. Its the industry-leader for automation, there are 880+ integrations, and it has the best drag-and-drop editor weve tested. With so many features, there is a bit of a learning curve but with a huge knowledge base and support team, its definitely worth your time.</li>
<li>Sendinblue  Offering SMS marketing as well as email marketing tools, Sendinblue has an affordable solution thats easy to use. It even has a generous free plan. You can create automated emails, add workflows, and use the option to send it at the best time.</li>
<li>AWeber  Offering a unique drag-and-drop campaign builder, AWeber gives you everything you need for successful email marketing. Its very beginner-friendly but still has more complex features, such as split-test functions and it can connect to more than 5000 apps with Zapier.</li>
<li><strong>Constant Contact </strong>&#8211; With hundreds of email templates to choose from and a 30-day free trial (60-day if youre in the US), Constant Contact is an excellent choice. Its great for creating automated emails, and its really easy to use, meaning you can get started right away.</li>
<li><strong>Benchmark Email </strong>&#8211; Supporting multiple languages, Benchmark Email is a top choice if your native language isnt English. It has a free plan, too, that lets you send up to 3,500 emails per month. Its great for beginners but has more advanced tools that you can use as you grow more familiar with the platform.</li>
<li><strong>GetResponse </strong>&#8211; More than just an email marketing platform, GetResponse is a multi-functional platform that incorporates marketing, customer relationship management (CRM), and webinar features. Theres a 30-day free trial, too.</li>
</ul>
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=2175&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_2175_post_4_771164&post_id=4&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=post&amp=0" data-id="2175" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_2175_post_4_771164', 'activecampaign', this,  true  );">Try ActiveCampaign for Free &gt;&gt;</a></div>
<h2 id="hselect--7"><strong>Final Words</strong></h2>
Phew! Thats a lot of information weve covered. To sum up, here are a few key takeaways from this guide to building your own website:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/website-builders/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Website builders</a></strong><strong></strong>are a great place to start when youre a beginner.<strong> Wix</strong>is one of the most flexible of them all, allowing you to start with the basics and add more advanced apps later.</li>
<li><strong>WordPress is often regarded as more difficult than website builders, but it offers much more freedom.</strong>Its also a cheaper way of getting your website online, with lots of low-cost <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/web-hosting/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">website hosting</a></strong>plans available.</li>
<li>If you dont have the time to build your website yourself, you can <strong>hire a developer on Fiverr for as little as $5</strong>. Who said working with a web developer had to break your budget?</li>
<li>Publishing your website isnt the end of the process. You can keep optimizing and promoting your website with tools for SEO, analytics, and marketing.</li>
</ul>
Anyone can build a website and it doesnt matter if youre a beginner or only have a tiny budget to spend. Have fun creating your website!</p>

                            <div class="new-post-row new-post-section-comments-item-content">Be careful who you hire on Fiverr to handle your website. I understand you probably have an affiliate partnership with them, but I know plenty of people who were burned by Fiverr web designers and developers. While I do believe you can create a cost-effective website without breaking the bank, relying on these low-tier services by usually underqualified freelancers always ends up costing you much more in the long run. </div>

    var datadog_logger_inited = false;

    function datadog_logger_init() {
        if (datadog_logger_inited) {
            return;
        }
        datadog_logger_inited = !0;
        DD_LOGS.init({
            clientToken: 'pubae90c910f262c6a56887a7ef8bb5c378',
            forwardErrorsToLogs: true,
        });

        for (var N = 0; N < vm_js_erros.length; N++) {
            DD_LOGS.logger.error("JS: " + vm_js_erros[N].message + " in " + vm_js_erros[N].file + " : " + vm_js_erros[N].line, {
                status: "error",
                error: vm_js_erros[N]
            });
        }
    }

    function load_datadog(e) {
        w.removeEventListener('scroll', load_datadog, !1);
        setTimeout(function() {
            if (datadog_logger_inited) {
                return;
            }
            var head = d.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
            var script = d.createElement('script');
            script.async = !0;
            script.type = 'text/javascript';
            script.src = "https://www.datadoghq-browser-agent.com/datadog-logs-us.js";
            script.onreadystatechange = datadog_logger_init;
            script.onload = datadog_logger_init;
            head.appendChild(script);
        }, 800);
    }
    w.addEventListener('scroll', load_datadog, false);
})(window, document);</script>
